	public static Dictionary<string, string> dict
	{
		get
		{
			return SimpleLocale._localeDictionary;
		}
		set
		{
			SimpleLocale._localeDictionary = value;
		}
	}
	public static string GetString(string key)
	{
		if (SimpleLocale._localeDictionary.ContainsKey(key))
		{
			return SimpleLocale._localeDictionary[key];
		}
		Watchdog.LogWarning("Translation Key \"" + key + "\" not found!");
		return key;
	}
}
